def disp():
    rist[27] = '〇'
    rist[28] = '●'
    rist[35] = '●'
    rist[36] = '〇'
    for i in range(64):
        print(rist[i],end='')
        if i%8 == 7:
            print()

def displ():
    for i in range(61):
        print(rist[i],end='')
        if i%8 == 7:
            print()
def reset(p):
    a = p+1
    button_(a).place_remove()


def katimake():
    if cnt == 61:
        B=rist.count('●')
        W=rist.count('〇')
        print(B,W)
        if B > W:
            messagebox.showinfo('結果',"●が勝ちました")
        elif W > B:
            messagebox.showinfo('結果',"〇が勝ちました")
            print(B,W)
        elif B == W:
            messagebox.showinfo('結果',"引き分けです")
    else:
        B=rist.count('●')
        W=rist.count('〇')
        print(B,W)

                                        canvas.create_oval(68,12+55*(n/8),112,56+55*(n/8),fill='Black')
                                        if v%8 == 0:
                                            canvas.create_oval(68,12+55*(v/8),112,56+55*(v/8),fill='Black')
                                        elif not v%8 == 0:
                                            canvas.create_oval(68+60*(v%8),12+55*(v//8),112+60*(v%8),56+55*(v//8),fill='Black')
                                    elif not n%8 == 0:
                                        canvas.create_oval(68+60*(n%8),12+55*(n//8),112+60*(n%8),56+55*(n//8),fill='Black')
                                        if v%8 == 0:
                                            canvas.create_oval(68,12+55*(v/8),112,56+55*(v/8),fill='Black')
                                        elif not v%8 == 0:
                                            canvas.create_oval(68+60*(v%8),12+55*(v//8),112+60*(v%8),56+55*(v//8),fill='Black')


    katimake()
    print(cnt)
    print(rist)
    print(p)
